                        "import requests\nimport threading\nimport time\nimport datetime\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# Configure logging\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s')\n\n# --- CONFIGURATION ---\n\nAPI_CONFIGS = [\n    {\n        \"name\": \"AlphaVantage\",\n        \"url\": \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\",\n        \"params\": {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": \"\",  # To be filled in\n            \"interval\": \"5min\",\n            \"apikey\": \"demo\"  # Replace with your API key\n        },\n        \"rate_limit_per_minute\": 5\n    },\n    # Add more APIs as needed\n]\n\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = [\"AAPL\", \"MSFT\", \"GOOG\"]  # Example symbols\n\nSCAN_TIMES = [\"09:35\", \"12:00\", \"15:45\"]  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- RATE LIMIT MANAGER ---\n\nclass RateLimitManager:\n    def __init__(self, rate_limit_per_minute: int):\n        self.rate_limit = rate_limit_per_minute\n        self.calls = []\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def can_call(self) -> bool:\n        with self.lock:\n            now = time.time()\n            # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n            self.calls = [call for call in self.calls if now - call < 60]\n            return len(self.calls) < self.rate_limit\n\n    def record_call(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            self.calls.append(time.time())\n\n# --- API FETCHER ---\n\nclass StockAPIClient:\n    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.config = config\n        self.rate_manager = RateLimitManager(config[\"rate_limit_per_minute\"])\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:\n        if not self.rate_manager.can_call():\n            logging.warning(f\"Rate limit exceeded for {self.config['name']}. Skipping {symbol}.\")\n            return None\n        params = self.config[\"params\"].copy()\n        params[\"symbol\"] = symbol\n        try:\n            response = requests.get(self.config[\"url\"], params=params, timeout=10)\n            self.rate_manager.record_call()\n            response.raise_for_status()\n            data = response.json()\n            # AlphaVantage returns data under \"Time Series (5min)\"\n            key = next((k for k in data if \"Time Series\" in k), None)\n            if key is None:\n                logging.error(f\"No time series data for {symbol} from {self.config['name']}.\")\n                return None\n            df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n            df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n            df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n            df = df.sort_index()\n            df = df.astype(float)\n            return df\n        except Exception as e:\n            logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol} from {self.config['name']}: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n# --- TECHNICAL INDICATORS ---\n\ndef calculate_sma(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef calculate_ema(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Exponential Moving Average\"\"\"\n    return series.ewm(span=window, adjust=False).mean()\n\ndef calculate_rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = np.where(delta > 0, delta, 0)\n    loss = np.where(delta < 0, -delta, 0)\n    avg_gain = pd.Series(gain).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = pd.Series(loss).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return pd.Series(rsi, index=series.index)\n\n# --- LOGIC APPLICATION ---\n\ndef apply_predefined_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Apply trading logic, e.g., crossovers and RSI thresholds\"\"\"\n    close = df[\"close\"]\n    df[\"SMA_20\"] = calculate_sma(close, 20)\n    df[\"EMA_20\"] = calculate_ema(close, 20)\n    df[\"RSI_14\"] = calculate_rsi(close, 14)\n\n    signals = []\n    for i in range(1, len(df)):\n        # Example logic: SMA/EMA crossover and RSI oversold/overbought\n        prev_sma = df[\"SMA_20\"].iloc[i-1]\n        prev_ema = df[\"EMA_20\"].iloc[i-1]\n        curr_sma = df[\"SMA_20\"].iloc[i]\n        curr_ema = df[\"EMA_20\"].iloc[i]\n        curr_rsi = df[\"RSI_14\"].iloc[i]\n        if np.isnan(curr_sma) or np.isnan(curr_ema) or np.isnan(curr_rsi):\n            continue\n        # Buy signal: EMA crosses above SMA and RSI < 30\n        if prev_ema < prev_sma and curr_ema > curr_sma and curr_rsi < 30:\n            signals.append({\"timestamp\": df.index[i], \"signal\": \"BUY\"})\n        # ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving averages\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\nfrom unittest import mock\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving averages\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\";                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving averages\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = None\n    if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n        signal = \"Bullish\"\n    elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n        signal = \"Bearish\"\n    else:\n        signal = \"Neutral\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        # Standard functionality\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        # Edge case: window larger than series length\n        ma_large = moving_average(self.close, 100)\n        self.assertTrue(ma_large.isna().all())\n        # Edge case: window = 1\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close.astype(float))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        # Standard functionality\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n        # Edge case: constant series\n        const_series = pd.Series([100] * 20)\n        rsi_const = rsi(const_series, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(rsi_const[14:], 0))\n        # Edge case: window larger than series length\n        rsi_large = rsi(self.close, 100)\n        self.assertTrue(rsi_large.isna().all())\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n        self.assertIsInstance(result['MA5'], float)\n        self.assertIsInstance(result['MA20'], float)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_edge(self):\n        # Edge case: not enough data for MA20/RSI14\n        data = {'close': [100, 101, 102]}\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n        result = apply_logic(df)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(result['MA20']))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(result['RSI14']))\n        self.assertEqual(result['Signal'], 'Neutral')\n\nclass TestRateLimiter(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_rate_limiter(self):\n        # Test that rate limiter does not sleep when under limit\n        rl = RateLimiter(3)\n        start = time.time()\n        for _ in range(3):\n            rl.wait()\n        duration = time.time() - start\n        self.assertLess(duration, 1)  # Should not sleep\n\n        # Test that rate limiter sleeps when over limit\n        rl = RateLimiter(2)\n        rl.call_times = [time.time() - 59, time.time() - 1]\n        start = time.time()\n        rl.wait()\n        duration = time.time() - start\n        self.assertGreaterEqual(duration, 0)  # Should sleep at least a bit\n\nclass TestAlphaVantageClient(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        self.client = AlphaVantageClient('demo', self.rate_limiter)\n\n    def test_fetch_intraday_success(self):\n        #                     "best_code": "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving averages\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = None\n    if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n        signal = \"Bullish\"\n    elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n        signal = \"Bearish\"\n    else:\n        signal = \"Neutral\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Keep only calls in the last 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving averages\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = None\n    if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n        signal = \"Bullish\"\n    elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n        signal = \"Bearish\"\n    else:\n        signal = \"Neutral\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n\nclass TestIntegration(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_alpha_vantage_client(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        # Standard functionality\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        # Edge case: Not enough data for window\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n        # Edge case: window = 1 (should return original series)\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close.astype(float))\n\n        # Edge case: window larger than series\n        ma_large = moving_average(self.close, 100)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all(np.isnan(ma_large)))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        # Standard functionality\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\n        # Edge case: window = 1 (should be all NaN except first value)\n        rsi1 = rsi(self.close, 1)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all(np.isnan(rsi1)))\n\n        # Edge case: constant series (should result in NaN for all)\n        const = pd.Series([100]*20)\n        rsi_const = rsi(const, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all(np.isnan(rsi_const)))\n\n        # Edge case: decreasing series (RSI should be low)\n        dec = pd.Series(np.arange(100, 80, -1))\n        rsi_dec = rsi(dec, 14)\n        # All should be NaN except last value, which should be close to 0\n        self.assertTrue(rsi_dec.iloc[-1] < 10 or np.isnan(rsi_dec.iloc[-1]))\n\n        # Edge case: increasing series (RSI should be high)\n        inc = pd.Series(np.arange(80, 100, 1))\n        rsi_inc = rsi(inc, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(rsi_inc.iloc[-1] > 90 or np.isnan(rsi_inc.iloc[-1]))\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Third call should sleep\n        rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertTrue(elapsed >= 0)  # Should not raise\n\n    def test_rate_limiter_edge(self):\n        rl = RateLimiter(1)\n        rl.wait()\n        # Next call should sleep for nearly 60 seconds\n        t0 = time.time()\n        rl.wait()\n        t1 = time.time()\n        self.assertTrue(t1 - t0 >= 0)  # Should not raise\n\nclass TestAlphaVantageClient(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        self.client = AlphaVantageClient('demo', self.rate_limiter)\n\n    def test_fetch_intraday_success(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        # Standard case\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n        # Edge case: window=1\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close)\n        # Edge case: window larger than series\n        ma_large = moving_average(self.close, len(self.close) + 1)\n        self.assertTrue(ma_large.isnull().all())\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        # Standard case\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n        # Edge case: constant series\n        rsi_const = rsi(pd.Series([100] * 20), 14)\n        self.assertTrue((rsi_const[13:] == 0).all() or (rsi_const[13:] == 100).all())\n        # Edge case: decreasing series\n        rsi_dec = rsi(pd.Series(range(120, 100, -1)), 14)\n        self.assertTrue((rsi_dec[13:] <= 50).all())\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        # Standard case\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        # Edge case: insufficient data for window\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n        # Edge case: window=1 should equal original series\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close.astype(float))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        # Edge case: insufficient data for RSI\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        # RSI should be between 0 and 100 for valid values\n        valid_rsi = rsi14.dropna()\n        self.assertTrue((valid_rsi >= 0).all() and (valid_rsi <= 100).all())\n        # Edge case: constant series returns NaN\n        const_series = pd.Series([100]*20)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi(const_series, 14).iloc[-1]))\n\n    def test_moving_average_empty(self):\n        # Edge case: empty series\n        empty = pd.Series([], dtype=float)\n        ma = moving_average(empty, 5)\n        self.assertEqual(len(ma), 0)\n\n    def test_rsi_empty(self):\n        # Edge case: empty series\n        empty = pd.Series([], dtype=float)\n        rsi_val = rsi(empty, 14)\n        self.assertEqual(len(rsi_val), 0)\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_nan(self):\n        # Edge case: DataFrame with insufficient data for indicators\n        short_df = pd.DataFrame({'close': [100, 101]}, index=pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=2, freq='5min'))\n        result = apply_logic(short_df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(result['MA5']) or np.isnan(result['MA20']) or np.isnan(result['RSI14']))\n\n    def test_apply_logic_constant(self):\n        # Third call should sleep\n        rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertGreaterEqual(elapsed, 0)\n        # Should not sleep if under limit\n        rl = RateLimiter(1000)\n        start = time.time()\n        for _ in range(10):\n            rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertLess(elapsed, 1)\n\nclass TestAlphaVantageClient(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_fetch_intraday_invalid_symbol(self):\n        rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        client = AlphaVantageClient('demo', rate_limiter)\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            client.fetch_intraday('INVALIDSYMBOL123')\n\n    def test_fetch_intraday_demo(self):\n        rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        client = AlphaVantageClient('demo', rate_limiter)\n        try:\n            df = client.fetch_intraday('IBM')\n            self.assertIn('close', df.columns)\n            self.assertGreater(len(df), 0)\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.fail(f\"AlphaVantageClient integration failed: {e}\")\n\nclass TestFinnhubClient(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_fetch_quote_invalid(self):\n        rate_limiter = RateLimiter(60)\n        client = FinnhubClient('', rate_limiter)\n        #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached.
