')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n\nclass TestIntegration(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_alpha_vantage_client(self):\n        # Integration test with AlphaVantage demo key\n        rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        client = AlphaVantageClient('demo', rate_limiter)\n        try:\n            df = client.fetch_intraday('IBM')\n            self.assertIn('close', df.columns)\n            self.assertGreater(len(df), 0)\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.fail(f\"AlphaVantageClient integration failed: {e}\")\n\n    def test_stock_scanner(self):\n        # Use AlphaVantage demo key for scanner\n        av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(5)\n        clients = {'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient('demo', av_rate_limiter)}\n        scanner = StockScanner(['IBM'], clients)\n        results = scanner.scan()\n        self.assertIn('IBM', results)\n        self.assertIn('Signal', results['IBM'])\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    import sys\n    if len(sys.argv) > 1 and sys.argv[1] == 'test':\n        unittest.main(argv=[sys.argv[0]])\n    else:\n        main()",
                        "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        \"\"\"\n        Fetch intraday time series data for a given symbol.\n        Returns a DataFrame with columns: open, high, low, close, volume.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        # Rename columns to remove '1. ' etc.\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        # Convert all columns to float\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Fetch real-time quote for a given symbol.\n        Returns a dict with keys: c (current), h (high), l (low), o (open), pc (prev close), t (timestamp)\n        \"\"\"\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Schedule the scanner to run at specified times each day.\n    \"\"\"\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average_typical(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n    def test_moving_average_window_1(self):\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close)\n\n    def test_moving_average_window_larger_than_series(self):\n        ma = moving_average(self.close, len(self.close) + 1)\n        self.assertTrue(ma.isna().all())\n\n    def test_rsi_typical(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\n    def test_rsi_constant_series(self):\n        const_series = pd.Series([50]*20)\n        rsi_val = rsi(const_series, 14)\n        # RSI should be NaN for first 13, then 0 for all (no gain/loss)\n        self.assertTrue(np.allclose(rsi_val.iloc[14:], 0, atol=1e-6) | np.isnan(rsi_val.iloc[14:]))\n\n    def test_rsi_monotonic_increasing(self):\n        inc_series = pd.Series(range(1, 21))\n        rsi_val = rsi(inc_series, 14)\n        # Should approach 100\n        self.assertGreaterEqual(rsi_val.iloc[-1], 90)\n\n    def test_rsi_monotonic_decreasing(self):\n        dec_series = pd.Series(range(20, 0, -1))\n        rsi_val = rsi(dec_series, 14)\n        # Should approach 0\n        self.assertLessEqual(rsi_val.iloc[-1], 10)\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_signal_in_output(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_nan_handling(self):\n        # Artificial bearish scenario: MA5 < MA20, RSI14 > 30\n        df = self.df.copy()\n        df['close'] = np.linspace(200, 100, len(df))\n        result = apply_logic(df)\n        self.assertEqual(result['Signal'], 'Bearish')\n\nclass TestRateLimiter(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_rate_limiter_allows_within_limit(self):\n        rl = RateLimiter(3)\n        start = time.time()\n        for _ in range(3):\n            rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertLess(elapsed, 1.0)  # Should not sleep\n\n    def test_rate_limiter_blocks_when_exceeding_limit(self):\n        rl = RateLimiter(2)\n        rl.call_times = [time.time() - 59, time.time() - 1]\n        start = time.time()\n        rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertGreaterEqual(elapsed, 0)  #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, self.assertGreaterEqual(t1 - t0, 0)  # Should not sleep long since calls are old\n\n    def test_rate_limiter_enforces_limit(self):\n        limiter = RateLimiter(2)\n        limiter.call_times =                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average_typical(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], np.mean(self.close.iloc[0:5]))\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(ma5.iloc[3]))\n\n    def test_moving_average_window1(self):\n        ma1 = moving_average(self.close, 1)\n        pd.testing.assert_series_equal(ma1, self.close)\n\n    def test_moving_average_window_greater_than_length(self):\n        ma = moving_average(self.close, len(self.close) + 1)\n        self.assertTrue(ma.isna().all())\n\n    def test_rsi_typical(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n\n    def test_rsi_flat_series(self):\n        flat = pd.Series([100] * 20)\n        rsi_flat = rsi(flat, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all((rsi_flat[14:] == 0) | (np.isnan(rsi_flat[14:]))))\n\n    def test_rsi_short_series(self):\n        short = pd.Series([100, 101])\n        rsi_short = rsi(short, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(rsi_short.isna().all())\n\nclass TestApplyLogic(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a DataFrame similar to AlphaVantage output\n        data = {\n            'close': [100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125]\n        }\n        index = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(data['close']), freq='5min')\n        self.df = pd.DataFrame(data, index=index)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_signal_in_output(self):\n        result = apply_logic(self.df)\n        self.assertIn(result['Signal'], ['Bullish', 'Bearish', 'Neutral'])\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= result['RSI14'] <= 100)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_missing_close_column(self):\n        df = self.df.drop(columns=['close'])\n        with self.assertRaises(KeyError):\n            apply_logic(df)\n\n    def test_apply_logic_short_df(self):\n        df = self.df.iloc[:10].copy()\n        result = apply_logic(df)\n        self.assertIn('Signal', result)\n        # Should still return a signal, even if some values are nan\n\nclass TestRateLimiter(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_rate_limiter_allows_calls(self):\n        rl = RateLimiter(3)\n        start = time.time()\n        for _ in range(3):\n            rl.wait()\n        elapsed = time.time() - start\n        self.assertLess(elapsed, 1.0)  # Should not sleep\n\n    def test_rate_limiter_blocks_on_limit(self):\n        rl = RateLimiter(2)\n        rl.call_times = [time.time() - 1, time.time() - 1]\n        start = time.time()\n        rl.wait()  #                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\nimport schedule\nimport logging\nimport unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nAPI_KEYS = {\n    'alphavantage': os.getenv('ALPHAVANTAGE_API_KEY', 'demo'),  # Replace 'demo' with your real key\n    'finnhub': os.getenv('FINNHUB_API_KEY', ''),\n}\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'alphavantage': {'calls_per_minute': 5},\n    'finnhub': {'calls_per_minute': 60},\n}\nSTOCK_SYMBOLS = ['AAPL', 'MSFT', 'GOOGL', 'TSLA', 'AMZN']\nSCAN_TIMES = ['09:30', '12:00', '15:30']  # HH:MM in 24h format\n\n# --- Logging Setup ---\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\n\n# --- API Clients ---\nclass RateLimiter:\n    \"\"\"Simple rate limiter for API calls.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, calls_per_minute: int):\n        self.calls_per_minute = calls_per_minute\n        self.call_times = []\n\n    def wait(self):\n        now = time.time()\n        # Remove calls older than 60 seconds\n        self.call_times = [t for t in self.call_times if now - t < 60]\n        if len(self.call_times) >= self.calls_per_minute:\n            sleep_time = 60 - (now - self.call_times[0])\n            logging.info(f\"Rate limit reached. Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    # Let the main thread run for demonstration (e.g., 10 minutes)\n    time.sleep(600)\n    logging.info(\"Main program finished.\")\n\n# --- Unit and Integration Tests ---\nclass TestTechnicalIndicators(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a sample close price series\n        self.close = pd.Series([100, 102, 101, 105, 107, 110, 108, 109, 111, 115, 117, 120, 119, 118, 121, 123, 125])\n\n    def test_moving_average(self):\n        ma5 = moving_average(self.close, 5)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(ma5.iloc[4], self.assertTrue(ma_large.isna().all())\n\n    def test_rsi(self):\n        rsi14 = rsi(self.close, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.isnan(rsi14.iloc[13]))\n        self.assertTrue(0 <= rsi14.iloc[-1] <= 100)\n        # Edge case: constant series\n        const_series = pd.Series([100]*20)\n        rsi_const = rsi(const_series, 14)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all((rsi_const.dropna() == 0) | (rsi_const.dropna() == 100) | (np.isnan(rsi_const.dropna()))))\n\n    def test_rsi_short_series(self):\n        # Edge case: series shorter than window\n        short_series = pd.Series([100, 101, Sleeping for {sleep_time:.2f} seconds.\")\n            time.sleep(max(sleep_time, 0))\n        self.call_times.append(time.time())\n\nclass AlphaVantageClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://www.alphavantage.co/query\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_intraday(self, symbol: str, interval: str = \"5min\", outputsize: str = \"compact\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"function\": \"TIME_SERIES_INTRADAY\",\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"interval\": interval,\n            \"apikey\": self.api_key,\n            \"outputsize\": outputsize,\n            \"datatype\": \"json\"\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        key = f\"Time Series ({interval})\"\n        if key not in data:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unexpected API response: {data}\")\n        df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(data[key], orient='index')\n        df = df.rename(columns=lambda x: x.split('. ')[1])\n        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)\n        df = df.sort_index()\n        df = df.astype(float)\n        return df\n\nclass FinnhubClient:\n    BASE_URL = \"https://finnhub.io/api/v1/quote\"\n\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str, rate_limiter: RateLimiter):\n        self.api_key = api_key\n        self.rate_limiter = rate_limiter\n\n    def fetch_quote(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        self.rate_limiter.wait()\n        params = {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"token\": self.api_key\n        }\n        response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params, timeout=30)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n\n# --- Technical Indicators ---\ndef moving_average(series: pd.Series, window: int) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Simple Moving Average.\"\"\"\n    return series.rolling(window=window).mean()\n\ndef rsi(series: pd.Series, window: int = 14) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Relative Strength Index.\"\"\"\n    delta = series.diff()\n    gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0.0)\n    loss = -delta.where(delta < 0, 0.0)\n    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=window, min_periods=window).mean()\n    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\n# --- Predefined Logic ---\ndef apply_logic(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Example logic:\n    - 5-period and 20-period moving average\n    - RSI(14)\n    - Signal: If MA5 > MA20 and RSI < 70, \"Bullish\"; If MA5 < MA20 and RSI > 30, \"Bearish\"; else \"Neutral\"\n    \"\"\"\n    close = df['close']\n    df['MA5'] = moving_average(close, 5)\n    df['MA20'] = moving_average(close, 20)\n    df['RSI14'] = rsi(close, 14)\n    latest = df.iloc[-1]\n    signal = \"Neutral\"\n    if pd.notna(latest['MA5']) and pd.notna(latest['MA20']) and pd.notna(latest['RSI14']):\n        if latest['MA5'] > latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] < 70:\n            signal = \"Bullish\"\n        elif latest['MA5'] < latest['MA20'] and latest['RSI14'] > 30:\n            signal = \"Bearish\"\n    return {\n        'MA5': latest['MA5'],\n        'MA20': latest['MA20'],\n        'RSI14': latest['RSI14'],\n        'Signal': signal\n    }\n\n# --- Scanning Process ---\nclass StockScanner:\n    def __init__(self, symbols: List[str], clients: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.symbols = symbols\n        self.clients = clients\n\n    def scan(self):\n        logging.info(\"Starting scan...\")\n        results = {}\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            try:\n                # Prefer AlphaVantage for intraday data\n                df = self.clients['alphavantage'].fetch_intraday(symbol)\n                logic_result = apply_logic(df)\n                results[symbol] = logic_result\n                logging.info(f\"{symbol}: {logic_result}\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logging.error(f\"Error fetching data for {symbol}: {e}\")\n                results[symbol] = {'error': str(e)}\n        return results\n\ndef run_scheduled_scans(scanner: StockScanner, scan_times: List[str]):\n    for scan_time in scan_times:\n        schedule.every().day.at(scan_time).do(scanner.scan)\n    logging.info(\"Scheduler started. Waiting for scan times...\")\n    while True:\n        schedule.run_pending()\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n# --- Main Program ---\ndef main():\n    # Initialize API clients with rate limiters\n    av_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['alphavantage']['calls_per_minute'])\n    fh_rate_limiter = RateLimiter(RATE_LIMITS['finnhub']['calls_per_minute'])\n    clients = {\n        'alphavantage': AlphaVantageClient(API_KEYS['alphavantage'], av_rate_limiter),\n        'finnhub': FinnhubClient(API_KEYS['finnhub'], fh_rate_limiter),\n    }\n    scanner = StockScanner(STOCK_SYMBOLS, clients)\n\n    # Start scanning in a separate thread so main thread is free for tests or other tasks\n    scan_thread = threading.Thread(target=run_scheduled_scans, args=(scanner, SCAN_TIMES), daemon=True)\n    scan_thread.start()\n\n    #
